<ul><li>SS Nikola Tesla，一艘<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%94%B1%E8%BD%AE" title="自由轮">自由轮</a>，1943年8月31日铺设，1943年9月25日下水，1947年从政府服务中出售，1970年报废</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E8.AE.A1.E7.AE.97.E6.9C.BA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="计算机">计算机</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="编辑章节：计算机"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="特斯拉 (微架构)" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Tesla (microarchitecture)"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89_(%E5%BE%AE%E6%9E%B6%E6%9E%84)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="特斯拉 (微架构)（页面不存在）">特斯拉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesla_(microarchitecture)" class="extiw" title="en:Tesla (microarchitecture)"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Tesla (microarchitecture)</span></a></span>）</span></span>，<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E4%BC%9F%E8%BE%BE" title="英伟达">英伟达</a>公司开发的一种显卡图形处理单元微架构</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E8.B4.A7.E5.B8.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="货币">货币</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="编辑章节：货币"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%97%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%A4%AB%E7%AC%AC%E7%BA%B3%E5%B0%94" title="南斯拉夫第纳尔">南斯拉夫第纳尔</a>1970年（雕像）和1993年之间的6种不同的纸币上印有特斯拉</li>
<li>100<a href="/wiki/%E5%A1%9E%E7%88%BE%E7%B6%AD%E4%BA%9E%E7%AC%AC%E7%B4%8D%E7%88%BE" title="塞尔维亚第纳尔">塞尔维亚第纳尔</a>的纸币上印有特斯拉</li>
<li>克罗地亚发行的1<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E5%88%86" title="欧分">欧分</a>、2欧分及5欧分硬币上铸有特斯拉</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E6.B8.B8.E6.88.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="游戏">游戏</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=56" title="编辑章节：游戏"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E7%BA%A2%E8%89%B2%E8%AD%A6%E6%88%92%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="红色警戒系列">红色警戒</a>》中，有以他名字命名的武器“特斯拉线圈”，也被译为“磁暴线圈”</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%BA%E5%AE%A2%E6%95%99%E6%A2%9D%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="刺客教条系列">刺客信条</a>2》中的“真相”指出，特斯拉拥有能给人类带来先进科技的4号金苹果，并计划让世界有用之不尽的能源，特斯拉因此成为圣殿骑士们（爱迪生等人）攻击的对象</li>
<li>线上游戏《王者之剑》中，副本“混沌之塔”有以他名字命名的怪物“特斯拉线圈”，以释放强力电击攻击玩家</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%8B%E5%9B%BD%E4%BF%9D%E5%8D%AB%E6%88%98%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%97" title="王国保卫战系列">王国保卫战系列</a>》中，由矮人工程师所制造以释放电击来攻击敌人的塔被命名为“特斯拉X104 (TESLA X104)”</li>
<li>游戏《<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="MouseHunt" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="MouseHunt"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=MouseHunt&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="MouseHunt（页面不存在）">MouseHunt</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MouseHunt" class="extiw" title="en:MouseHunt"><span lang="en" dir="auto">MouseHunt</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中，一款限量版的捕鼠陷阱被称为“Chesla Revenge”。Chesla意指Cheese（乳酪）与Tesla（特斯拉）。它释放强大的电力来攻击老鼠</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E7%B5%95%E5%9C%B0%E8%A6%81%E5%A1%9E2" title="绝地要塞2">军团要塞2</a>》的官方数位漫画中提及，特斯拉为1850年代的蓝组工程师，并使用一袋蓝图以建造辅助建筑物</li>
<li>手机游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E9%83%A8%E8%90%BD%E5%86%B2%E7%AA%81" title="部落冲突">部落冲突</a>》、《皇室战争》中，有以他名字命名的建筑设备“特斯拉电磁塔”</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/The_Order:_1886" class="mw-redirect" title="The Order: 1886">The Order: 1886</a>》中，提供主角的团队各种武器</li>
<li>手机游戏《勇者的盆栽》Heroes Flick中，有以他和摩根的故事作蓝本的角色 - 科研之子达士拿</li>
<li>手机游戏《<a href="/wiki/Fate/Grand_Order" title="Fate/Grand Order">Fate/Grand Order</a>》中，以“Archer”的职阶登场，拥有EX宝具“人类神话‧雷电降临”</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E9%AC%A5%E9%99%A3%E7%89%B9%E6%94%BB" title="斗阵特攻">守望先锋</a>》中，猩猩科学家“Winston”所使用的武器电机枪被命名为“特斯拉电磁炮”</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/Robocraft" title="Robocraft">Robocraft</a>》中，创建机器人的装备选项有“特斯拉刀”</li>
<li>游戏《<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="They Are Billions" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="They Are Billions"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=They_Are_Billions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="They Are Billions（页面不存在）">They Are Billions</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/They_Are_Billions" class="extiw" title="en:They Are Billions"><span lang="en" dir="auto">They Are Billions</span></a></span>）</span></span>》中有功能为无线输电的“特斯拉塔”</li>
<li>手机游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A2%E7%95%8C%E7%89%A9%E8%AA%9E" title="梦界物语">梦界物语</a>》中其中一位导灵</li>
<li>手机游戏《造物法则》中主角夜北的载体（主角夜北的前载体为爱迪生，后为特斯拉）</li>
<li>手机游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E5%B4%A9%E5%A3%9E3rd" class="mw-redirect" title="崩坏3rd">崩坏3rd</a>》中的登场角色及圣痕，改编自现实的特斯拉</li>
<li>游戏《<a href="/wiki/%E8%8D%92%E9%87%8E%E5%A4%A7%E9%95%96%E5%AE%A2%EF%BC%9A%E6%95%91%E8%B5%8E2" class="mw-redirect" title="荒野大镖客：救赎2">荒野大镖客：救赎2</a>》中，有他的支线故事〈聪明的天才男孩〉，在1898年，特斯拉曾展示可远端操控的船模通过无线电波来操作螺旋桨和灯光，当时船模配有多块大号电池以及无线电信号控制器远端控制（或远端自动化）的理念至今也被人们广为应用</li>
<li>手机游戏《CODE:SEED 星火之歌》中的一名攻击型游戏角色，特斯拉 模组为3D角色并攻击招式都为电系招式</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E5.BD.B1.E8.A6.96.E4.BD.9C.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="影視作品">影视作品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="编辑章节：影视作品"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>2006年电影《<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%B4%E5%91%BD%E9%AD%94%E6%9C%AF" class="mw-redirect" title="致命魔术">致命魔术</a>》提到特斯拉，片中他发明的放大发射器能够多次复制各种物体（包括生命体）</li>
<li>2008年电影《<a href="/wiki/K20%EF%BC%9A%E6%80%AA%E4%BA%BA%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E9%9D%A2%E7%9B%B8" title="K20：怪人二十面相">K20：怪人二十面相</a>》中虚构出特斯拉的“特斯拉装置”。该装置可以使电器不借助电线便运行起来，比如在数米之外运行特斯拉装置，可以使一颗没有放入台灯中的台灯灯泡发光</li>
<li>2008年电视剧《<a href="/wiki/%E7%95%B0%E5%BD%A2%E5%BA%87%E8%AD%B7%E6%89%80" title="异形庇护所">异形庇护所</a>》中，他被描述为拥有血族的天才科学家，由于注射远古血族的血液而觉醒为世界上最后一个血族（特裔）</li>
<li>2015年电影《<a href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E6%97%A5%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C_(%E7%94%B5%E5%BD%B1)" title="明日世界 (电影)">明日世界</a>》将特斯拉与<a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" class="mw-redirect" title="爱迪生">爱迪生</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%89%BE%E8%8F%B2%E7%88%BE" class="mw-redirect" title="埃菲尔">埃菲尔</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E5%87%A1%E5%B0%94%E7%BA%B3" class="mw-redirect" title="凡尔纳">凡尔纳</a>视为明日世界的创造者</li>
<li>2019年电影《<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%B5%81%E5%A4%A7%E6%88%B0_(%E9%9B%BB%E5%BD%B1)" title="电流大战 (电影)">电流大战</a>》描述<a href="/wiki/%E4%B9%94%E6%B2%BB%C2%B7%E5%A8%81%E6%96%AF%E6%B1%80%E8%B1%AA%E6%96%AF" title="乔治·威斯汀豪斯">乔治·威斯汀豪斯</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" class="mw-redirect" title="爱迪生">爱迪生</a>为争取美国最大供电商的称号所引发的商业竞争</li>
<li>2020年电影《<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89_(2020%E5%B9%B4%E9%9B%BB%E5%BD%B1)" title="特斯拉 (2020年电影)">特斯拉</a>》描述特斯拉的生平故事，包括交流电的发明以及与<a href="/wiki/%E6%84%9B%E8%BF%AA%E7%94%9F" class="mw-redirect" title="爱迪生">爱迪生</a>的激烈对抗</li>
<li>2020年电视剧《<a href="/wiki/%E7%95%B0%E4%B8%96%E5%A5%87%E4%BA%BA_(%E7%B3%BB%E5%88%9712)" title="异世奇人 (系列12)">神秘博士</a>》第十二季第四集《尼古拉·特斯拉惊魂夜》中，特斯拉偶然发现一外星记录仪并对其回复信息，信息被另一外星种族截获，后者的女王以地球生命安危要挟特斯拉为其修理损坏的太空飞船</li></ul>
<h4><span id=".E6.BC.AB.E7.95.AB.E4.BD.9C.E5.93.81"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="漫畫作品">漫画作品</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=58" title="编辑章节：漫画作品"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>漫画《造物法则》中作为主角的载体登场</li>
<li>漫画《<a href="/wiki/%E7%B5%82%E6%9C%AB%E7%9A%84%E5%A5%B3%E6%AD%A6%E7%A5%9E" title="终末的女武神">终末的女武神</a>》中作为人类参战方之一的斗士</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參見">参见</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=59" title="编辑章节：参见"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="特斯拉電燈與製造公司" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E9%9B%BB%E7%87%88%E8%88%87%E8%A3%BD%E9%80%A0%E5%85%AC%E5%8F%B8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="特斯拉电灯与制造公司（页面不存在）">特斯拉电灯与制造公司</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tesla_Electric_Light_and_Manufacturing" class="extiw" title="en:Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Tesla Electric Light and Manufacturing</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="List of things named after Nikola Tesla"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BB%A5%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%91%BD%E5%90%8D%E7%9A%84%E4%BA%8B%E7%89%A9%E6%B8%85%E5%8D%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单（页面不存在）">以尼古拉·特斯拉命名的事物清单</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_things_named_after_Nikola_Tesla" class="extiw" title="en:List of things named after Nikola Tesla"><span lang="en" dir="auto">List of things named after Nikola Tesla</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Nikola Tesla in popular culture"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%A4%A7%E4%BC%97%E6%96%87%E5%8C%96%E4%B8%AD%E7%9A%84%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉（页面不存在）">大众文化中的尼古拉·特斯拉</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nikola_Tesla_in_popular_culture" class="extiw" title="en:Nikola Tesla in popular culture"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Nikola Tesla in popular culture</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%A5%E7%88%BE%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%99%AE%E7%BE%85%E9%80%8F%E6%96%AF%C2%B7%E6%96%AF%E6%B3%B0%E5%9B%A0%E6%A2%85%E8%8C%A8" title="查尔斯·普罗透斯·斯泰恩梅茨">查尔斯·普罗透斯·斯泰恩梅茨</a>——同时代的交流电和高电压研究的电气先锋</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E7%B1%B3%E9%AB%98%C2%B7%E6%B3%95%E6%8B%89%E7%AC%AC" class="mw-redirect" title="米高·法拉第">迈克尔·法拉第</a></li></ul>

<h2><span id=".E6.B3.A8.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B0%BC%E5%8F%A4%E6%8B%89%C2%B7%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="编辑章节：注释"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="notelist" style="list-style-type: lower-alpha;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-31"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-31">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">特斯拉没有提到这是哪位教授的名字，但一些资料认为这是<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="马丁·塞库利奇" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Martin Sekulić"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%A9%AC%E4%B8%81%C2%B7%E5%A1%9E%E5%BA%93%E5%88%A9%E5%A5%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="马丁·塞库利奇（页面不存在）">马丁·塞库利奇</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Martin_Sekuli%C4%87" class="extiw" title="en:Martin Sekulić"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Martin Sekulić</span></a></span>）</span></span>教授。</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-131"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-131">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：Within the room were suspended two hard-rubber plates covered with tin foil. These were about fifteen feet apart and served as terminals of the wires leading from the transformers. When the current was turned on, the lamps or tubes, which had no wires connected to them, but lay on a table between the suspended plates, or which might be held in the hand in almost any part of the room, were made luminous. These were the same experiments and the same apparatus shown by Tesla in London about two years previous, "where they produced so much wonder and astonishment".</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-212"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-212">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：I have been feeding pigeons, thousands of them for years. But there was one, a beautiful bird, pure white with light grey tips on its wings; that one was different. It was a female. I had only to wish and call her and she would come flying to me. I loved that pigeon as a man loves a woman, and she loved me. As long as I had her, there was a purpose to my life.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-235"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-235">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：His [Tesla's] thoughts and efforts during at least the past 15 years were primarily of a speculative, philosophical, and somewhat promotional character often concerned with the production and wireless transmission of power; but did not include new, sound, workable principles or methods for realizing such results.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-263"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-263">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：He had no hobby, cared for no sort of amusement of any kind and lived in utter disregard of the most elementary rules of hygiene ... His method was inefficient in the extreme, for an immense ground had to be covered to get anything at all unless blind chance intervened and, at first, I was almost a sorry witness of his doings, knowing that just a little theory and calculation would have saved him 90 percent of the labor. But he had a veritable contempt for book learning and mathematical knowledge, trusting himself entirely to his inventor's instinct and practical American sense.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-274"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-274">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：I hold that space cannot be curved, for the simple reason that it can have no properties. It might as well be said that God has properties. He has not, but only attributes and these are of our own making. Of properties we can only speak when dealing with matter filling the space. To say that in the presence of large bodies space becomes curved is equivalent to stating that something can act upon nothing. I, for one, refuse to subscribe to such a view.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-280"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-280">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">原文：... man's new sense of pity began to interfere with the ruthless workings of nature. The only method compatible with our notions of civilization and the race is to prevent the breeding of the unfit by sterilization and the deliberate guidance of the mating instinct ... The trend of opinion among eugenists is that we must make marriage more difficult. Certainly no one who is not a desirable parent should be permitted to produce progeny. A century from now it will no more occur to a normal person to mate with a person eugenically unfit than to marry a habitual criminal.</span>
</li>
</ol>
</div>

<p><b>书籍</b>
</p>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r80540462"><div class="refbegin" style="">
<ul><li>Tesla, Nikola, <i><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="My Inventions" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="My Inventions"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=My_Inventions&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="My Inventions（页面不存在）">My Inventions</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/My_Inventions" class="extiw" title="en:My Inventions"><span lang="en" dir="auto">My Inventions</span></a></span>）</span></span>,</i> Parts I through V published in the <i>Electrical Experimenter</i> monthly magazine from February through June 1919. Part VI published October 1919. Reprint edition with introductory notes by Ben Johnson, New York: Barnes and Noble, 1982; also online at <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" <ul><li><span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="特斯拉專利列表" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="List of Nikola Tesla patents"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%89%B9%E6%96%AF%E6%8B%89%E5%B0%88%E5%88%A9%E5%88%97%E8%A1%A8&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="特斯拉专利列表（页面不存在）">专利</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_Nikola_Tesla_patents" class="extiw" title="en:List of Nikola Tesla patents"><span lang="en" dir="auto">List of Nikola Tesla patents</span></a></span>）</span></span></li>
